\DoxyCodeLine{1302 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1303 \textcolor{comment}{/* Specialization for reference-\/counted types. This depends on the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1304 \textcolor{comment}{ * existence of Wrapper<T>::cl\_type, and none of the other types having the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1305 \textcolor{comment}{ * cl\_type member. Note that simplify specifying the parameter as Wrapper<T>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1306 \textcolor{comment}{ * does not work, because when using a derived type (e.g. Context) the generic}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1307 \textcolor{comment}{ * template will provide a better match.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1308 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1309 \textcolor{keyword}{template}<\textcolor{keyword}{typename} Func, \textcolor{keyword}{typename} T>}
\DoxyCodeLine{1310 \textcolor{keyword}{inline} cl\_int getInfoHelper(Func f, cl\_uint name, T* param, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}, \textcolor{keyword}{typename} T::cl\_type = 0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1311 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1312     \textcolor{keyword}{typename} T::cl\_type value;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1313     cl\_int err = f(name, \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(value), \&value, NULL);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1314     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (err != CL\_SUCCESS) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1315         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} err;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1316     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1317     *param = value;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1318     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (value != NULL)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1319     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1320         err = param-\/>retain();}
\DoxyCodeLine{1321         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (err != CL\_SUCCESS) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1322             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} err;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1323         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1324     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1325     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} CL\_SUCCESS;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1326 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1327 }

\DoxyCodeLine{1771 \textcolor{comment}{// Extracts version number with major in the upper 16 bits, minor in the lower 16}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1772 \textcolor{keyword}{static} cl\_uint getVersion(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *versionInfo)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1773 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1774     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} highVersion = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1775     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} lowVersion = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1776     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} index = 7;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1777     \textcolor{keywordflow}{while}(versionInfo[index] != \textcolor{charliteral}{'.'} ) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1778         highVersion *= 10;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1779         highVersion += versionInfo[index]-\/\textcolor{charliteral}{'0'};}
\DoxyCodeLine{1780         ++index;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1781     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1782     ++index;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1783     \textcolor{keywordflow}{while}(versionInfo[index] != \textcolor{charliteral}{' '} \&\&  versionInfo[index] != \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)0'}) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1784         lowVersion *= 10;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1785         lowVersion += versionInfo[index]-\/\textcolor{charliteral}{'0'};}
\DoxyCodeLine{1786         ++index;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1787     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1788     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} (highVersion << 16) | lowVersion;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1789 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1790 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1791 \textcolor{keyword}{static} cl\_uint getPlatformVersion(cl\_platform\_id platform)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1792 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1793     ::size\_t size = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1794     clGetPlatformInfo(platform, CL\_PLATFORM\_VERSION, 0, NULL, \&size);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1795     \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *versionInfo = (\textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *) alloca(size);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1796     clGetPlatformInfo(platform, CL\_PLATFORM\_VERSION, size, \&versionInfo[0], \&size);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1797     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} getVersion(versionInfo);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1798 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1799 }

\DoxyCodeLine{1807 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if defined(CL\_VERSION\_1\_2) \&\& defined(CL\_USE\_DEPRECATED\_OPENCL\_1\_1\_APIS)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1808 \textcolor{keyword}{static} cl\_uint getContextPlatformVersion(cl\_context context)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1809 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1810     \textcolor{comment}{// The platform cannot be queried directly, so we first have to grab a}}
